style="page-break-after:always"/><div style="min-height:42.75pt;width:100%"><div><span><br/></span></div></div><div><span style="color:#000000;font-family:'Times New Roman',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:700;line-height:120%">Item 2.02 Results of Operations and Financial Condition. </span></div><div><span><br/></span></div><div><span style="color:#000000;font-family:'Times New Roman',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">The information provided under Item 8.01 below is incorporated by reference to this Item 2.02 in its entirety.</span></div><div><span><br/></span></div><div><span style="color:#000000;font-family:'Times New Roman',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:700;line-height:120%">Item 8.01 Other Events.</span></div><div><span><br/></span></div><div><span style="color:#000000;font-family:'Times New Roman',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:400;line-height:112%">As part of the global transition away from the London Interbank Offered Rate as a benchmark rate, various alternative reference rates were established, including the Bloomberg Short-Term Bank Yield Index (&#8220;BSBY&#8221;) and Secured Overnight Financing Rate (&#8220;SOFR&#8221;). Beginning in 2021, Bank of America Corporation (the &#8220;Corporation&#8221;) and other members of the banking industry began utilizing these rates in various lending agreements, including commercial loans.  </span></div><div><span><br/></span></div><div><span style="color:#000000;font-family:'Times New Roman',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:400;line-height:112%">On November 15, 2023, the Bloomberg Index Services Limited announced that the permanent cessation of BSBY and all its tenors will be effective on November 15, 2024. After such announcement, and following the Corporation&#8217;s internal and external consultations, it was determined that the accounting transition relief in ASC 848, </span><span style="color:#000000;font-family:'Times New Roman',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-style:italic;font-weight:400;line-height:112%">Reference Rate Reform</span><span style="color:#000000;font-family:'Times New Roman',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:400;line-height:112%">, is not available for BSBY cessation</span><span style="background-color:#ffffff;color:#000000;font-family:'Times New Roman',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:400;line-height:112%">. </span></div><div><span><br/></span></div><div><span style="background-color:#ffffff;color:#000000;font-family:'Times New Roman',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:400;line-height:112%">Accordingly, under </span><span style="color:#000000;font-family:'Times New Roman',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:400;line-height:112%">U.S. GAAP, the Corporation was required to &#8220;de-designate&#8221; certain interest rate swaps used in cash flow hedges of certain BSBY-indexe&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;d loans, as of November 15, 2023, and reclassify into earnings any amounts recognized in the accumulated other comprehensive income category of shareholders&#8217; equity that relate to forecasted cash flows that are now no longer expected to occur.</span><span style="background-color:#ffffff;color:#000000;font-family:'Times New Roman',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:400;line-height:112%"> Therefore, the Corporation recognized a net non-cash, pretax charge of approximately $</span><span style="color:#000000;font-family:'Times New Roman',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:400;line-height:112%">1.6 </span><span style="background-color:#ffffff;color:#000000;font-family:'Times New Roman',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:400;line-height:112%">billion in the quarter ending December 31, 2023 (the &#8220;Charge&#8221;) presented in revenue through market making and similar activities</span><span style="color:#000000;font-family:'Times New Roman',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:400;line-height:112%">. The $1.6 billion net impact is expected to be recognized back into the Corporation&#8217;s interest income in subsequent periods largely through 2026. The impact of such accounting treatment is solely due to the expectation that interest payments on the BSBY-indexed loans will change to SOFR, which is expected to have a nominal impact to the economics of these loans. </span><span style="background-color:#ffffff;color:#000000;font-family:'Times New Roman',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:400;line-height:112%">The Charge reduced the Corporation&#8217;s common equity tier 1 (CET1) ratio by eight basis points, as of December 31, 2023</span><span style="color:#000000;font-family:'Times New Roman',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:400;line-height:112%">.  </span></div><div><span><br/></span></div><div><span style="color:#000000;font-family:'Times New Roman',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:400;line-height:112%">The Corporation </span><span style="background-color:#ffffff;color:#000000;font-family:'Times New Roman',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:400;line-height:112%">will report its fourth-quarter 2023 financial results on Friday, January 12, 2024</span><span style="color:#000000;font-family:'Times New Roman',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:400;line-height:112%">. </span></div><div><span><br/></span></div><div><span style="color:#000000;font-family:'Times New Roman',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:700;line-height:115%">Forward-Looking Statements</span></div><div><span style="color:#000000;font-family:'Times New Roman',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">Certain statements contained in this Report may constitute &#8220;forward-looking&#8221; statements within the meaning of the Private Securities Litigation Reform Act of 1995. These forward-looking statements represent the current expectations, plans or forecasts of the Corporation based on available information. Forward-looking statements can be identified by the fact that they do not relate strictly to historical or current facts. e.removeAttribute('id');a.parentNode.appendChild(e)}}
if(e)e.style.display='block';Show.LastAR=e};Show.hideAR=function(){Show.LastAR.style.display='none'};Show.toggleNext=function(a){var e=a;while(e.nodeName!='DIV')e=e.nextSibling;if(!e.style){}else if(!e.style.display){}else{var d,p_;if(e.style.display=='none'){d='block';p='-'}else{d='none';p='+'}
e.style.display=d;if(a.textContent){a.textContent=p+a.textContent.substring(1)}else{a.innerText=p+a.innerText.substring(1)}}}
